name	equation	unit	description
_sTime_	_sTime_ = _time_	_day_	Time
_TimeYears_	_TimeYears_ = _sTime_ / _DaysPerYear_	_yr_	Time_in_years
_Day_	_Day_ = _sTime_ - _FLOOR_(_TimeYears_) * _DaysPerYear_	_-_	Time_(day_number)_within_the_year_(0-365)
_Years_	_Years_ = _YearZero_ + _TimeYears_	_yr_	Time_in_calendar_years
_uTm_	_uTm_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclSeason_) _THEN_ _cTmAve_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadTemp_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mTemp_ _ELSE_ _cTmAve_ - _cTmVar_ * _COS_(2.0*_Pi_*(_sTime_ + _TenDays_ - _cTimeLag_) / _DaysPerYear_) _ENDIF_	_oC_	Forcing_function_temperature
_uVWind_	_uVWind_ = _IF_ (_ReadVWind_ _EQ_ _TRUE_)_THEN_ _mVWind_ _ELSE_ _cVWind_ _ENDIF_	_m_/_sec_	Forcing_function_wind_speed
_ufDay_	_ufDay_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclSeason_) _THEN_ _cfDayAve_ _ELSE_ _cfDayAve_ - _cfDayVar_ * _COS_(2.0*_Pi_*(_sTime_+_TenDays_) / _DaysPerYear_) _ENDIF_	_hr_/_day_	Day_length
_uLDay_	_uLDay_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclSeason_) _THEN_ _cLDayAve_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadLOut_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSE_ _cLDayAve_ - _cLDayVar_ * _COS_(2.0*_Pi_*(_sTime_+_TenDays_) / _DaysPerYear_) _ENDIF_	_J_/_m2_/_day_	Total_daily_radiation
_uLOut_	_uLOut_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclSeason_) _THEN_ _uLDay_ / _SecsPerDay_ / _ufDay_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadLOut_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mLOut_ / _ufDay_ _ELSE_ _uLDay_ / _SecsPerDay_ / _ufDay_ _ENDIF_	_W_/_m2_	Average_light_intensity_during_daytime

_aExtDet_	_aExtDet_ = _cExtSpDet_ * _sDDetW_	1/_m_	Detrital_contribution_to_extinction

_uQEvSinus_	_uQEvSinus_ = _cQEvAve_ - _cQEvVar_ * _COS_(2.0*_Pi_ * (_sTime_ + _TenDays_ - _cTimeLag_) / _DaysPerYear_)	_mm_/_day_	Sinusoid_evaporation
_uQEv_	_uQEv_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclSeason_) _THEN_ _cQEvAve_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadQEv_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mQEv_ _ELSE_ _uQEvSinus_ _ENDIF_	_mm_/_day_	Evaporation
_uQInExtra_	_uQInExtra_ = _IF_ ((_Day_ _GE_ _cDayApril1_ - 0.5*_cLengChange_) _AND_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayApril1_ + 0.5*_cLengChange_)) _THEN_ _cQInExtraApril1_ _ELSEIF_ ( (_Day_ _GE_ _cDayOct1_ - 0.5*_cLengChange_) _AND_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayOct1_ + 0.5*_cLengChange_) ) _THEN_ _cQInExtraOct1_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_mm_/_day_	Extra_inflow_(for_periodic_water_level_regulation

_uQOut_	_uQOut_ = _IF_ (_ReadQOut_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _MAX_(_mQOut_, (_sDepthW_ - _cDepthWMax_) * _mmPerm_) _ELSE_ _MAX_(0.0, (_uQIn_ - _uQInExtra_) - _uQEv_ - _cQInf_) + _uQOutExtra_ _ENDIF_	_mm_/_day_	Outflow

_akExchM_	_akExchM_ = _IF_ (_InclMarsh_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _fMarsh_ _GT_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ _kExchMaxM_ * _hfMarsh_ /(_hfMarsh_ + _fMarsh_) + _vTranDepthW_ / _sDepthWM_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_m3_/_m3marsh_/_day_	Marsh_water_exchange_coefficient

_iPPulse_	_iPPulse_ = 1	_-_	-
_uPLoadSeason_	_uPLoadSeason_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _UseSeasonLoad_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayApril1_ - 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ _cPLoadWin_ _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayApril1_ + 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ 0.5*(_cPLoadWin_ + _cPLoadSum_) + 0.5*(_cPLoadWin_ - _cPLoadSum_) * _COS_(_Pi_/_cLengChange_ * (_Day_ - _cDayApril1_)) _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayOct1_ - 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ _cPLoadSum_ _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayOct1_ + 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ 0.5*(_cPLoadWin_ + _cPLoadSum_) - 0.5*(_cPLoadWin_ - _cPLoadSum_) * _COS_(_Pi_/_cLengChange_ * (_Day_ - _cDayOct1_)) _ELSE_ _cPLoadWin_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Seasonal_P_load
_uPLoad_	_uPLoad_ = _IF_ (_ReadPLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mPLoadPO4_ + _mPLoadOrg_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadPLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadNutFrac_) _THEN_ _mPLoad_ _ELSEIF_ (_UsePulseLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_UseSeasonLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _uPLoadSeason_ _ELSE_ _cPLoad_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	P_load
_uPLoadPO4_	_uPLoadPO4_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadPLoad_) _THEN_ _fPO4In_ * _uPLoad_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mPLoadPO4_ _ELSE_ _fPO4In_ * _mPLoad_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	P_load_PO4
_uPLoadOrg_	_uPLoadOrg_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadPLoad_) _THEN_ (1.0 - _fPO4In_) * _uPLoad_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mPLoadOrg_ _ELSE_ (1.0 - _fPO4In_) * _mPLoad_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	P_load_bound_to_org_matter
_uPLoadPhytTot_	_uPLoadPhytTot_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclSeason_) _THEN_ (((_fPhytInSum_ + _fPhytInWin_)/2)*_uPLoadOrg_) _ELSEIF_ (_ReadPLoadPhyt_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mPLoadPhytTot_ _ELSE_ ((_fPhytInSum_+_fPhytInWin_)/2.0 - (_fPhytInSum_-_fPhytInWin_)/2.0 * _COS_(2.0*_Pi_ * (_sTime_ + _TenDays_ - _cTimeLag_) / _DaysPerYear_)) * _uPLoadOrg_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	(total)_algal_P_input
_uPLoadDet_	_uPLoadDet_ = _uPLoadOrg_ - _uPLoadPhytTot_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Detrital_P_input
_uPLoadAIM_	_uPLoadAIM_ = 0.0	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Adsorbed_P_loading_(=0)
_iNPulse_	_iNPulse_ = 1	_-_	-
_uNLoadSeason_	_uNLoadSeason_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _UseSeasonLoad_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayApril1_ - 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ _cNLoadWin_ _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayApril1_ + 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ 0.5*(_cNLoadWin_ + _cNLoadSum_) + 0.5*(_cNLoadWin_ - _cNLoadSum_) * _COS_(_Pi_/_cLengChange_ * (_Day_ - _cDayApril1_)) _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayOct1_ - 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ _cNLoadSum_ _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayOct1_ + 0.5*_cLengChange_) _THEN_ 0.5*(_cNLoadWin_ + _cNLoadSum_) - 0.5*(_cNLoadWin_ - _cNLoadSum_) * _COS_(_Pi_/_cLengChange_ * (_Day_ - _cDayOct1_)) _ELSE_ _cNLoadWin_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Seasonal_N_load
_uNLoadPhytTot_	_uNLoadPhytTot_ = _cNPPhytIn_ * _uPLoadPhytTot_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	(total)_algal_N_input
_uNLoad_	_uNLoad_ = _IF_ (_ReadNLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mNLoadNH4_ + _mNLoadNO3_ + _mNLoadOrg_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadNutFrac_) _THEN_ _mNLoad_ _ELSEIF_ (_UsePulseLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_ReadPLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _cNPLoadMeas_ * _uPLoad_ _ELSEIF_ (_UseSeasonLoad_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _uNLoadSeason_ _ELSE_ _cNLoad_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	N_load
_uNLoadDet_	_uNLoadDet_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadNLoad_) _THEN_ _MIN_(_cNPDetIn_ * _uPLoadDet_, _uNLoad_ - _uNLoadPhytTot_) _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSE_ _MIN_(_cNPDetIn_ * _uPLoadDet_, _uNLoad_ - _uNLoadPhytTot_) _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	N_load_detritus
_uNLoadOrg_	_uNLoadOrg_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadNLoad_) _THEN_ _uNLoadPhytTot_ + _uNLoadDet_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mNLoadOrg_ _ELSE_ _uNLoadPhytTot_ + _uNLoadDet_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Loading_N_bound_to_org_matter
_uNLoadDiss_	_uNLoadDiss_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadNLoad_) _THEN_ _uNLoad_ - _uNLoadOrg_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSE_ _uNLoad_ - _uNLoadOrg_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	N_loading_dissolved_(sum_of_NO2_and_NH4)
_uNLoadNH4_	_uNLoadNH4_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadNLoad_) _THEN_ _fNH4DissIn_ * _uNLoadDiss_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mNLoadNH4_ _ELSE_ _fNH4DissIn_ * _uNLoadDiss_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	NH4_loading
_uNLoadNO3_	_uNLoadNO3_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _ReadNLoad_) _THEN_ (1.0 - _fNH4DissIn_) * _uNLoadDiss_ _ELSEIF_ (_ReadNutFrac_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mNLoadNO3_ _ELSE_ (1.0 - _fNH4DissIn_) * _uNLoadDiss_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	NO3_loading
_uNTotIn_	_uNTotIn_ = _uNLoad_ / (_uQIn_ / _mmPerm_ + _NearZero_)	_mgN_/_l_	External_N_conc
_uDLoadDet_	_uDLoadDet_ = _IF_ (_ReadDLoadDet_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mDLoadDet_ _ELSE_ _uNLoadDet_ / _cNDDetIn_ _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Detrital_DW_loading
_uDLoadPhytTot_	_uDLoadPhytTot_ = _uNLoadPhytTot_ / _cNDPhytIn_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	(total)_algal_DW_input
_uDLoadIM_	_uDLoadIM_ = _IF_ (_ReadDLoadIM_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _mDLoadIM_ _ELSE_ _cDIMIn_ * _uQIn_ / _mmPerm_ _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Loading_of_DW_of_inorg_matter
_uDLoad_	_uDLoad_ = _uDLoadIM_ + _uDLoadDet_ + _uDLoadPhytTot_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Total_DW_input
_uPTotIn_	_uPTotIn_ = _uPLoad_ / (_uQIn_ / _mmPerm_ + _NearZero_)	_gP_/_m3_	External_P_concentration

_wO2MinDetW_	_wO2MinDetW_ = _molO2molC_ * _cCPerDW_ * _aCorO2BOD_ * _wDMinDetW_	_gO2_/_m3_/_day_	O2_flux_due_to_mineralization_of_detritus

_aCorO2NitrW_	_aCorO2NitrW_ = _sO2W_*_sO2W_ / (_hO2Nitr_*_hO2Nitr_ + _sO2W_*_sO2W_)	_-_	Oxygen_consumption_during_nitrification

_uFunTmMinS_	_uFunTmMinS_ = _POW_(_cThetaMinS_ _POWOPERATOR_ (_uTm_-_cTmRef_))	_-_	Temp_function
_tDMinDetS_	_tDMinDetS_ = _kDMinDetS_ * _uFunTmMinS_ * _sDDetS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Decomposition_of_upper_sediment

_tSOD_	_tSOD_ = (_molO2molC_ * _cCPerDW_ * (1.0 - _fRefrDetS_) * _tDMinDetS_ + _O2PerNH4_ * _molO2molN_ * _kNitrS_ * _uFunTmNitr_ * _sNH4S_) / _cDepthS_	_gO2_/_m3_/_day_	Sediment_oxygen_demand
_aDepthOxySed_	_aDepthOxySed_ = _POW_((2.0 * _sO2W_ * _akO2DifCor_ / _tSOD_) _POWOPERATOR_ (0.5))	_m_	Oxygen_penetration_depth
_afOxySed_	_afOxySed_ = _aDepthOxySed_ / _cDepthS_	_-_	Fraction_aerobic_sediment
_tDMinOxyDetS_	_tDMinOxyDetS_ = _afOxySed_ * (1.0 - _fRefrDetS_) * _tDMinDetS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Aerobic_mineralisation

_tNDenitS_	_tNDenitS_ = _NO3PerC_ * _molNmolC_ * _cCPerDW_ * _tDDenitS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Denitrification_flux

_tO2NitrS_	_tO2NitrS_ = _O2PerNH4_ * _molO2molN_ * _tNNitrS_	_gO2_/_m2_/_day_	O2_flux_due_to_nitrification

_aDepthDif_	_aDepthDif_ = _fDepthDifS_ * _cDepthS_	_m_	Average_diffusion_distance
_tPDifPO4_	_tPDifPO4_ = _kPDifPO4_ * _uFunTmDif_ * _cTurbDifNut_ * _bPorCorS_ * (_oPO4S_ - _sPO4W_ ) / _aDepthDif_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Diffusion_flux_of_dissolved_P_from_sediment_to_water

_aPAdsMaxW_	_aPAdsMaxW_ = _cRelPAdsD_ + _aCorO2BOD_ * _cRelPAdsFe_ * _fFeDIM_ + _cRelPAdsAl_ * _fAlDIM_	_gP_/_gDW_	Max_P_adsorption_per_g_inorg_matter_in_water
_aKPAdsW_	_aKPAdsW_ = (1.0 - _fRedMax_ * (1.0-_aCorO2BOD_)) * _cKPAdsOx_	_m3_/_gP_	P_adsorption_affinity_corrected_for_redox_conditions

_wPSorpIMW_	_wPSorpIMW_ = _kPSorp_ * (_aPEqIMW_ - _sPAIMW_)	_gP_/_m3_/_day_	Sorption_flux_in_water
_aPAdsMaxS_	_aPAdsMaxS_ = _cRelPAdsD_ + _afOxySed_ * _cRelPAdsFe_ * _fFeDIM_ + _cRelPAdsAl_ * _fAlDIM_	_gP_/_gDW_	Max_P_adsorption_per_g_inorg_matter_in_sediment
_aKPAdsS_	_aKPAdsS_ = (1.0 - _fRedMax_ * (1.0-_afOxySed_)) * _cKPAdsOx_	_m3_/_gP_	P_adsorption_affinity_corrected_for_redox_conditions

_wDAbioIMW_	_wDAbioIMW_ = (_uDErosIMW_ - _tDSetIM_ + _tDResusIM_) / _sDepthW_	_gDW_/_m3_/_day_	Total_abiotic/microbial_DW_inorganic_matter_flux_in_water

_tPInfPO4WM_	_tPInfPO4WM_ = _IF_ (_InclMarsh_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _fMarsh_ _GT_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_cQInf_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _cQInf_ / _mmPerm_ * _sPO4WM_ _ELSE_ _cQInf_ / _mmPerm_ * _oPO4SM_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Infiltr_of_SRP

_tNInfNO3WM_	_tNInfNO3WM_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclMarsh_ _OR_ _fMarsh_ _LE_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_cQInf_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _cQInf_ / _mmPerm_ * _sNO3WM_ _ELSE_ _cQInf_ / _mmPerm_ * _oNO3SM_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Infiltr_of_nitrate

_tNInfNO3SM_	_tNInfNO3SM_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclMarsh_ _OR_ _fMarsh_ _LE_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_cQInf_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _cQInf_ / _mmPerm_ * _oNO3SM_ _ELSE_ _cQInf_ / _mmPerm_ * _oNO3SM_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Infiltration_of_interst_NO3

_bfRootVeg_	_bfRootVeg_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclSeason_) _THEN_ _fRootVegSum_ _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _aDayInitVeg_) _THEN_ _fRootVegWin_ _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _aDayInitVeg_ + _cLengAllo_) _THEN_ 0.5*(_fRootVegWin_ + _fRootVegSum_) + 0.5*(_fRootVegWin_ - _fRootVegSum_) * _COS_(_Pi_/_cLengAllo_ * (_Day_ - _aDayInitVeg_)) _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayWinVeg_) _THEN_ _fRootVegSum_ _ELSEIF_ (_Day_ _LT_ _cDayWinVeg_ + _cLengAllo_) _THEN_ 0.5*(_fRootVegWin_ + _fRootVegSum_) - 0.5*(_fRootVegWin_ - _fRootVegSum_) * _COS_(_Pi_/_cLengAllo_ * (_Day_ - _cDayWinVeg_)) _ELSE_ _fRootVegWin_ _ENDIF_	_-_	Setting_root_fration
_bfShootVeg_	_bfShootVeg_ = 1.0 - _bfRootVeg_	_-_	Shoot_fraction
_aDRootVeg_	_aDRootVeg_ = _bfRootVeg_ * _sDVeg_	_g_/_m2_	Root_biomass
_aDShootVeg_	_aDShootVeg_ = _bfShootVeg_ * _sDVeg_	_g_/_m2_	Shoot_biomass

_aDFloatVeg_	_aDFloatVeg_ = _fFloatVeg_ * _aDShootVeg_	_g_/_m2_	Floating_biomass
_bfSubVeg_	_bfSubVeg_ = 1.0 - _fFloatVeg_ - _fEmergVeg_	_-_	Submerged_fraction_of_shoot
_aDSubVeg_	_aDSubVeg_ = _bfSubVeg_ * _aDShootVeg_	_g_/_m2_	Submerged_biomass
_aExtVeg_	_aExtVeg_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclBed_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSE_ _cExtSpVeg_ * _aDSubVeg_ / _sDepthW_ _ENDIF_	1/_m_	Contribution_of_plant_species_to_extinction_(submerged)
_aDepth1Veg_	_aDepth1Veg_ = _fDepth1Veg_ * _sDepthW_	_m_	Upper_depth_of_vegetation_layer_(minimum_=_0_m_=_surface)
_aDepth2Veg_	_aDepth2Veg_ = _fDepth2Veg_ * _sDepthW_	_m_	Lower_depth_of_vegetation_layer_(maximum_=_water_depth)
_afCovSurfVeg_	_afCovSurfVeg_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _InclBed_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSE_ _MIN_(1.0, _MAX_(_aDFloatVeg_ / (_cDLayerVeg_ + _NearZero_), _aDEmergVeg_ / (_fEmergVeg_ * _cDCarrVeg_ + _NearZero_) ) ) _ENDIF_	_-_	Fraction_of_water_SURFACE_covered_by_plant_species
_afCovEmergVeg_	_afCovEmergVeg_ = _MIN_(1.0, _PerCent_ * _cCovSpVeg_ * _aDEmergVeg_)	_-_	Fraction_emergent_coverage
_aCovVeg_	_aCovVeg_ = _MIN_(100.0, _cCovSpVeg_ * _aDShootVeg_)	_-_	Percent_cover
_aDVeg_	_aDVeg_ = _sDVeg_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Total_plant_biomass
_aPVeg_	_aPVeg_ = _sPVeg_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Total_P_in_vegetation
_aNVeg_	_aNVeg_ = _sNVeg_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Total_N_in_vegetation
_aExtCoef_	_aExtCoef_ = _aExtCoefOpen_ + _aExtVeg_	1/_m_	Extinction_coefficient_incl_vegetation

_afPUptVegS_	_afPUptVegS_ = _IF_ (_FALSE_ _EQ_ _UseEmpUpt_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_bfRootVeg_ _LE_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSEIF_ (_fFloatVeg_ + _bfSubVeg_ _LE_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ 1.0 _ELSE_ _fSedUptVegMax_ / (1.0 + _fSedUptVegCoef_ * _POW_(((_oPO4S_+_NearZero_) / (_sPO4W_+_NearZero_)) _POWOPERATOR_ _fSedUptVegExp_)) _ENDIF_	_-_	Fraction_of_P_uptake_from_sediment

_uFunTmGren_	_uFunTmGren_ = _EXP_(-0.5/(_cSigTmGren_*_cSigTmGren_) *((_uTm_-_cTmOptGren_)*(_uTm_-_cTmOptGren_) - (_cTmRef_-_cTmOptGren_)*(_cTmRef_-_cTmOptGren_)))	_-_	Temperature_function_of_Algae
_uFunTmProdGren_	_uFunTmProdGren_ = _uFunTmGren_	_-_	Temperature_function_of_Algae
_uFunTmRespGren_	_uFunTmRespGren_ = _uFunTmGren_	_-_	Temperature_function_of_Algae
_aVPUptMaxCrGren_	_aVPUptMaxCrGren_ = _MAX_(0.0,_cVPUptMaxGren_ * _uFunTmProdGren_ *(_cPDGrenMax_ - _rPDGrenW_) /(_cPDGrenMax_ - _cPDGrenMin_))	_-_	Maximum_P_uptake_rate_of_Algae_corrected_for_P/D_ratio
_aVPUptGren_	_aVPUptGren_ = _sPO4W_ * _aVPUptMaxCrGren_ /(_aVPUptMaxCrGren_ / _cAffPUptGren_ + _sPO4W_)	_mgP_/_mgDW_/_day_	P_uptake_rate_of_Algae
_wPUptGren_	_wPUptGren_ = _aVPUptGren_ * _sDGrenW_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	P_uptake_Algae
_aVNUptMaxCrGren_	_aVNUptMaxCrGren_ = _MAX_(0.0,_cVNUptMaxGren_ * _uFunTmProdGren_ * (_cNDGrenMax_ - _rNDGrenW_) /(_cNDGrenMax_ - _cNDGrenMin_))	_-_	Maximum_N_uptake_rate_of_Algae_corrected_for_N/D_ratio
_ahNUptGren_	_ahNUptGren_ = _aVNUptMaxCrGren_ / _cAffNUptGren_	_mgN_/_l_	Half-sat_NDissW_for_uptake_by_Algae
_aVNUptGren_	_aVNUptGren_ = _oNDissW_ * _aVNUptMaxCrGren_ /(_ahNUptGren_ + _oNDissW_)	_mgN_/_mgDW_/_day_	N_uptake_rate_of_Algae
_wNUptGren_	_wNUptGren_ = _aVNUptGren_ * _sDGrenW_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	N_uptake_Algae
_afNH4UptGren_	_afNH4UptGren_ = _sNH4W_ * _sNO3W_ /((_ahNUptGren_ + _sNH4W_) *(_ahNUptGren_ + _sNO3W_)) + _sNH4W_ * _ahNUptGren_ /((_sNH4W_ + _sNO3W_) *(_ahNUptGren_ + _sNO3W_))	_-_	Fraction_ammonium_uptake_by_Algae
_wNUptNH4Gren_	_wNUptNH4Gren_ = _afNH4UptGren_ * _wNUptGren_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Ammonium_uptake_by_Algae
_wNUptNO3Gren_	_wNUptNO3Gren_ = _wNUptGren_ - _wNUptNH4Gren_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Nitrate_uptake_by_Algae
_uMuMaxTmGren_	_uMuMaxTmGren_ = _cMuMaxGren_ * _uFunTmProdGren_	1/_day_	Max_growth_rate_of_Algae_at_ambient_temperature
_aPLimGren_	_aPLimGren_ = _MAX_(0.0,(1.0 - _cPDGrenMin_ / _rPDGrenW_) * _cPDGrenMax_ /(_cPDGrenMax_ - _cPDGrenMin_))	_-_	Droop_function(P)_for_Algae
_aNLimGren_	_aNLimGren_ = _MAX_(0.0,(1.0 - _cNDGrenMin_ / _rNDGrenW_) * _cNDGrenMax_ /(_cNDGrenMax_ - _cNDGrenMin_))	_-_	Droop_function(N)_for_Algae
_aSiLimGren_	_aSiLimGren_ = _sSiO2W_ /(_hSiAssGren_ + _sSiO2W_)	_-_	Silica_dependence_of_growth_rate
_aLLimGren_	_aLLimGren_ = _UseSteeleGren_ *(_EXP_(1.0) /(_aExtCoef_ * _sDepthW_) *(_EXP_(- _aLPARBot_ /(_cLOptRefGren_ * _uFunTmProdGren_)) - _EXP_(- _uLPARSurf_ /(_cLOptRefGren_ * _uFunTmProdGren_)))) +(1.0 - _UseSteeleGren_) *(1.0 /(_aExtCoef_ * _sDepthW_) * _LN_((1.0 + _uLPARSurf_ / (_hLRefGren_ * _uFunTmProdGren_)) / (1.0 + _aLPARBot_ /(_hLRefGren_ * _uFunTmProdGren_))))	_-_	Light_function
_aMuTmLGren_	_aMuTmLGren_ = _ufDay_ *(1.0 - _afCovSurfVeg_) * _aLLimGren_ * _uMuMaxTmGren_	1/_day_	Growth_rate_at_current_light_AND_temp
_aNutLimGren_	_aNutLimGren_ = _MIN_(_aPLimGren_,(_MIN_(_aNLimGren_,_aSiLimGren_)))	1/_day_	Nutrient_limitation_function_of_Algae
_aMuGren_	_aMuGren_ = _aNutLimGren_ * _aMuTmLGren_	1/_day_	Growth_rate
_wDAssGren_	_wDAssGren_ = _aMuGren_*_sDGrenW_	_gDW_/_m3_/_day_	Assimilation_Algae
_rChDGren_	_rChDGren_ = _cChDGrenMax_ -(_cChDGrenMax_ - _cChDGrenMin_) * _aLLimGren_	_mg_/_mg_	Chlorophyll-a/DW_ratio_Algae
_oChlaGren_	_oChlaGren_ = _mgPerg_ * _rChDGren_ * _sDGrenW_	_mg_/_m3_	Chlorophyll-a_conc
_aExtChGren_	_aExtChGren_ = _cExtSpGren_ / _rChDGren_	_m2_/_mgchl-a_	Specific_extinction_per_unit_chlorophyll-a
_ukDRespTmGren_	_ukDRespTmGren_ = _kDRespGren_ * _uFunTmRespGren_	1/_day_	Temp_corrected_respiration_constant_of_Algae
_wDRespGrenW_	_wDRespGrenW_ = _ukDRespTmGren_ * _sDGrenW_	_g_/_m2_/_day_	Respiration_of_Algae_in_water
_ukLossTmGren_	_ukLossTmGren_ = _UseLoss_ * _kLossGren_ * _uFunTmLoss_	1/_day_	Daily_grazing_on_Algae
_wDLossGren_	_wDLossGren_ = _ukLossTmGren_ * _sDGrenW_	_mgDW_/_l_/_day_	Algae_grazing_loss
_wDMortGrenW_	_wDMortGrenW_ = _kMortGrenW_ * _sDGrenW_	_g_/_m3_/_day_	Mortality_in_water
_uCorVSetGren_	_uCorVSetGren_ = _cVSetGren_ * _aFunTauSetOM_ * _uFunTmSet_	_m_/_day_	Corrected_sedimentation_velocity_of_Algae
_tDSetGren_	_tDSetGren_ = _uCorVSetGren_ * _sDGrenW_	_g_/_m2_/_day_	Sedimentation_flux_of_Algae
_tDResusGren_	_tDResusGren_ = _sDGrenS_ /(_aDPhytS_+_NearZero_) * _tDResusPhytTot_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Resuspension_of_Algae
_tDRespGrenS_	_tDRespGrenS_ = _ukDRespTmGren_ * _sDGrenS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Respiration_of_sediment_Algae
_tDMortGrenS_	_tDMortGrenS_ = _kMortGrenS_ * _sDGrenS_	_g_/_m2_/_day_	Mortality_in_sed
_ukDDecGren_	_ukDDecGren_ = _ukDRespTmGren_ + _ukLossTmGren_ + _kMortGrenW_ +(_uCorVSetGren_ * _uFunTmSet_) / _sDepthW_	1/_day_	Total_loss_rate_of_algae_in_water(excl_dilution)
_wPExcrGrenW_	_wPExcrGrenW_ = (2.0 *_rPDGrenW_) /(_cPDGrenMax_ + _rPDGrenW_) * _rPDGrenW_ * _wDRespGrenW_	_gP_/_m3_/_day_	P_excretion_Algae_in_water
_wPLossGren_	_wPLossGren_ = _rPDGrenW_ * _wDLossGren_	_mgP_/_l_/_day_	Algae_grazing_loss
_wPMortGrenW_	_wPMortGrenW_ = _kMortGrenW_ * _sPGrenW_	_gP_/_m3_/_day_	Mortality_Algae_in_water
_tPSetGren_	_tPSetGren_ = _rPDGrenW_ * _tDSetGren_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Sedimentation
_tPResusGren_	_tPResusGren_ = _rPDGrenS_ * _tDResusGren_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Resuspension_of_algae
_tPExcrGrenS_	_tPExcrGrenS_ = (2.0 * _rPDGrenS_) /(_cPDGrenMax_ + _rPDGrenS_) * _rPDGrenS_ * _tDRespGrenS_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	P_excretion_of_algae_in_sediment
_tPMortGrenS_	_tPMortGrenS_ = _kMortGrenS_ * _sPGrenS_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	P_mortality_of_algae_in_sediment
_wNExcrGrenW_	_wNExcrGrenW_ = (2.0 * _rNDGrenW_) /(_cNDGrenMax_ + _rNDGrenW_) * _rNDGrenW_ * _wDRespGrenW_	_gN_/_m3_/_day_	N_excretion_Algae_in_water
_wNLossGren_	_wNLossGren_ = _rNDGrenW_ * _wDLossGren_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Algae_grazing_loss
_wNMortGrenW_	_wNMortGrenW_ = _kMortGrenW_ * _sNGrenW_	_gN_/_m3_/_day_	Mortality_Algae_in_water
_tNSetGren_	_tNSetGren_ = _rNDGrenW_ * _tDSetGren_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Sedimentation
_tNResusGren_	_tNResusGren_ = _rNDGrenS_ * _tDResusGren_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Resuspension_of_algae
_tNExcrGrenS_	_tNExcrGrenS_ = (2.0 * _rNDGrenS_) /(_cNDGrenMax_ + _rNDGrenS_) * _rNDGrenS_ * _tDRespGrenS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	N_excretion_of_algae_in_sediment
_tNMortGrenS_	_tNMortGrenS_ = _kMortGrenS_ * _sNGrenS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	N_mortality_of_algae_in_sediment
_wDPrimGrenW_	_wDPrimGrenW_ = _wDAssGren_ - _wDRespGrenW_ - _wDLossGren_ - _wDMortGrenW_ -(_tDSetGren_ - _tDResusGren_) / _sDepthW_	_mgDW_/_l_/_day_	Total_PRIM_flux_to_algae_in_water
_wPPrimGrenW_	_wPPrimGrenW_ = _wPUptGren_ - _wPExcrGrenW_ - _wPLossGren_ - _wPMortGrenW_ -(_tPSetGren_ - _tPResusGren_) / _sDepthW_	_mgP_/_l_/_day_	Total_PRIM_flux_to_Algae
_wNPrimGrenW_	_wNPrimGrenW_ = _wNUptGren_ - _wNExcrGrenW_ - _wNLossGren_ - _wNMortGrenW_ -(_tNSetGren_ - _tNResusGren_) / _sDepthW_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Total_PRIM_flux_to_Algae
_tDPrimGrenS_	_tDPrimGrenS_ = _IF_ (_InclPhytS_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _tDSetGren_ - _tDResusGren_ - _tDMortGrenS_ - _tDRespGrenS_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Total_flux_from_PRIM_module_to_sediment_Algae
_tPPrimGrenS_	_tPPrimGrenS_ = _IF_ (_InclPhytS_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _tPSetGren_ - _tPResusGren_ - _tPMortGrenS_ - _tPExcrGrenS_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Total_flux_from_PRIM_module_to_sediment_Algae
_tNPrimGrenS_	_tNPrimGrenS_ = _IF_ (_InclPhytS_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _tNSetGren_ - _tNResusGren_ - _tNMortGrenS_ - _tNExcrGrenS_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Total_flux_from_PRIM_module_to_sediment_Algae
_rPDDiatW_	_rPDDiatW_ = _sPDiatW_ /(_sDDiatW_+_NearZero_)	_-_	P/D_ratio_of_Algae
_rNDDiatW_	_rNDDiatW_ = _sNDiatW_ /(_sDDiatW_+_NearZero_)	_-_	N/D_ratio_of_Algae
_rPDDiatS_	_rPDDiatS_ = _sPDiatS_ /(_sDDiatS_+_NearZero_)	_-_	P/D_ratio_of_Algae
_rNDDiatS_	_rNDDiatS_ = _sNDiatS_ /(_sDDiatS_+_NearZero_)	_-_	N/D_ratio_of_Algae
_uFunTmDiat_	_uFunTmDiat_ = _EXP_(-0.5/(_cSigTmDiat_*_cSigTmDiat_) *((_uTm_-_cTmOptDiat_)*(_uTm_-_cTmOptDiat_) - (_cTmRef_-_cTmOptDiat_)*(_cTmRef_-_cTmOptDiat_)))	_-_	Temperature_function_of_Algae
_uFunTmProdDiat_	_uFunTmProdDiat_ = _uFunTmDiat_	_-_	Temperature_function_production_of_Algae
_uFunTmRespDiat_	_uFunTmRespDiat_ = _uFunTmDiat_	_-_	Temperature_function_respiration_of_Algae
_aVPUptMaxCrDiat_	_aVPUptMaxCrDiat_ = _MAX_(0.0,_cVPUptMaxDiat_ * _uFunTmProdDiat_ *(_cPDDiatMax_ - _rPDDiatW_) /(_cPDDiatMax_ - _cPDDiatMin_))	_-_	Maximum_P_uptake_rate_of_Algae_corrected_for_P/D_ratio
_aVPUptDiat_	_aVPUptDiat_ = _sPO4W_ * _aVPUptMaxCrDiat_ /(_aVPUptMaxCrDiat_ / _cAffPUptDiat_ + _sPO4W_)	_mgP_/_mgDW_/_day_	P_uptake_rate_of_Algae
_wPUptDiat_	_wPUptDiat_ = _aVPUptDiat_ * _sDDiatW_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	P_uptake_Algae
_aVNUptMaxCrDiat_	_aVNUptMaxCrDiat_ = _MAX_(0.0,_cVNUptMaxDiat_ * _uFunTmProdDiat_ * (_cNDDiatMax_ - _rNDDiatW_) /(_cNDDiatMax_ - _cNDDiatMin_))	_-_	Maximum_N_uptake_rate_of_Algae_corrected_for_N/D_ratio
_ahNUptDiat_	_ahNUptDiat_ = _aVNUptMaxCrDiat_ / _cAffNUptDiat_	_mgN_/_l_	Half-sat_NDissW_for_uptake_by_Algae

_wNUptDiat_	_wNUptDiat_ = _aVNUptDiat_ * _sDDiatW_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	N_uptake_Algae
_afNH4UptDiat_	_afNH4UptDiat_ = _sNH4W_ * _sNO3W_ /((_ahNUptDiat_ + _sNH4W_) *(_ahNUptDiat_ + _sNO3W_)) + _sNH4W_ * _ahNUptDiat_ /((_sNH4W_ + _sNO3W_) *(_ahNUptDiat_ + _sNO3W_))	_-_	Fraction_ammonium_uptake_by_Algae
_wNUptNH4Diat_	_wNUptNH4Diat_ = _afNH4UptDiat_ * _wNUptDiat_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Ammonium_uptake_by_Algae
_wNUptNO3Diat_	_wNUptNO3Diat_ = _wNUptDiat_ - _wNUptNH4Diat_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Nitrate_uptake_by_Algae
_uMuMaxTmDiat_	_uMuMaxTmDiat_ = _cMuMaxDiat_ * _uFunTmProdDiat_	1/_day_	Max_growth_rate_of_Algae_at_ambient_temperature
_aPLimDiat_	_aPLimDiat_ = _MAX_(0.0,(1.0 - _cPDDiatMin_ / _rPDDiatW_) * _cPDDiatMax_ /(_cPDDiatMax_ - _cPDDiatMin_))	_-_	Droop_function(P)_for_Algae
_aNLimDiat_	_aNLimDiat_ = _MAX_(0.0,(1.0 - _cNDDiatMin_ / _rNDDiatW_) * _cNDDiatMax_ /(_cNDDiatMax_ - _cNDDiatMin_))	_-_	Droop_function(N)_for_Algae
_aSiLimDiat_	_aSiLimDiat_ = _sSiO2W_ /(_hSiAssDiat_ + _sSiO2W_)	_-_	Silica_dependence_of_growth_rate

_aMuTmLDiat_	_aMuTmLDiat_ = _ufDay_ *(1.0 - _afCovSurfVeg_) * _aLLimDiat_ * _uMuMaxTmDiat_	1/_day_	Growth_rate_at_current_light_AND_temp
_aNutLimDiat_	_aNutLimDiat_ = _MIN_(_aPLimDiat_,(_MIN_(_aNLimDiat_,_aSiLimDiat_)))	1/_day_	Nutrient_limitation_function_of_Algae

_wDMortDiatW_	_wDMortDiatW_ = _kMortDiatW_ * _sDDiatW_	_g_/_m3_/_day_	Mortality_in_water
_uCorVSetDiat_	_uCorVSetDiat_ = _cVSetDiat_ * _aFunTauSetOM_ * _uFunTmSet_	_m_/_day_	Corrected_sedimentation_velocity_of_Algae
_tDSetDiat_	_tDSetDiat_ = _uCorVSetDiat_ * _sDDiatW_	_g_/_m2_/_day_	Sedimentation_flux_of_Algae

_tDMortDiatS_	_tDMortDiatS_ = _kMortDiatS_ * _sDDiatS_	_g_/_m2_/_day_	Mortality_in_sed

_wPExcrDiatW_	_wPExcrDiatW_ = (2.0 * _rPDDiatW_) /(_cPDDiatMax_ + _rPDDiatW_) * _rPDDiatW_ * _wDRespDiatW_	_gP_/_m3_/_day_	P_excretion_Algae_in_water

_wNExcrDiatW_	_wNExcrDiatW_ = (2.0 * _rNDDiatW_) /(_cNDDiatMax_ + _rNDDiatW_) * _rNDDiatW_ * _wDRespDiatW_	_gN_/_m3_/_day_	N_excretion_Algae_in_water
_wNLossDiat_	_wNLossDiat_ = _rNDDiatW_ * _wDLossDiat_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Algae_grazing_loss
_wNMortDiatW_	_wNMortDiatW_ = _kMortDiatW_ * _sNDiatW_	_gN_/_m3_/_day_	Mortality_Algae_in_water
_tNSetDiat_	_tNSetDiat_ = _rNDDiatW_ * _tDSetDiat_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Sedimentation

_aPACoef_	_aPACoef_ = _cPACoefMin_ +(_cPACoefMax_ - _cPACoefMin_) * _hPACoef_ / (_hPACoef_ + _oDOMW_)	_-_	Poole-Atkins_coefficient
_bSecchiMax_	_bSecchiMax_ = _sDepthW_ + _cSecchiPlus_	_m_	Max_Secchi_depth
_aSecchi_	_aSecchi_ = _MIN_(_bSecchiMax_,_aPACoef_ / _aExtCoefOpen_)	_m_	Secchi_depth
_aTransparency_	_aTransparency_ = _aSecchi_ / _sDepthW_	_m_	Secchi_depth
_aDepthEuph_	_aDepthEuph_ = _cEuph_ * _aSecchi_	_m_	Euphotic_depth
_aRelDepthEuph_	_aRelDepthEuph_ = _aDepthEuph_ / _sDepthW_	_m_	Relative_euphotic_depth
_aChlaH_	_aChlaH_ = _oChla_ * _sDepthW_	_mgchl-a_/_m2_	Chla_per_m2

_uFunTmZoo_	_uFunTmZoo_ = _EXP_(-0.5/(_cSigTmZoo_*_cSigTmZoo_) *((_uTm_-_cTmOptZoo_)*(_uTm_-_cTmOptZoo_) -(_cTmRef_-_cTmOptZoo_)*(_cTmRef_-_cTmOptZoo_)))	_-_	Temp_function_of_zooplankton
_rPDZoo_	_rPDZoo_ = _sPZoo_ /(_sDZoo_+_NearZero_)	_mgP_/_mgDW_	P/D_ratio_herbzooplankton
_rNDZoo_	_rNDZoo_ = _sNZoo_/(_sDZoo_+_NearZero_)	_mgN_/_mgDW_	N/C_ratio_herbzooplankton
_oDFoodZoo_	_oDFoodZoo_ = _cPrefDiat_ * _sDDiatW_ + _cPrefGren_ * _sDGrenW_ + _cPrefBlue_ * _sDBlueW_ + _cPrefDet_ * _sDDetW_	_mgDW_/_l_	Food_for_zooplankton
_aFilt_	_aFilt_ = _cFiltMax_ * _uFunTmZoo_ * _hFilt_ /(_hFilt_ + _oDOMW_)	_l_/_mgDW_/_day_	Filtering_rate
_ukDAssTmZoo_	_ukDAssTmZoo_ = _fDAssZoo_ * _cFiltMax_ * _uFunTmZoo_ * _hFilt_	1/_day_	Max_assimilation_rate_of_zooplanktontemp_corrected
_aDSatZoo_	_aDSatZoo_ = _oDFoodZoo_ /(_hFilt_ + _oDOMW_)	_-_	Food_saturation_function_of_zooplankton
_ukDRespTmZoo_	_ukDRespTmZoo_ = _kDRespZoo_ * _uFunTmZoo_	1/_day_	Respiration_constant_of_zooplankton
_ukDIncrZoo_	_ukDIncrZoo_ = _ukDAssTmZoo_ - _ukDRespTmZoo_ - _kMortZoo_	1/_day_	Intrinsic_rate_of_increase_of_zooplankton
_wDEnvZoo_	_wDEnvZoo_ = _MAX_(0.0,_ukDIncrZoo_ / _cDCarrZoo_ * _sDZoo_*_sDZoo_)	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Environmental_correction_of_zooplankton
_wDAssZoo_	_wDAssZoo_ = _aDSatZoo_ *(_ukDAssTmZoo_ * _sDZoo_ - _wDEnvZoo_)	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Assimilation_of_zooplankton
_wDConsZoo_	_wDConsZoo_ = _wDAssZoo_ / _fDAssZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Consumption_of_zooplankton
_wDConsDetZoo_	_wDConsDetZoo_ = _cPrefDet_*_sDDetW_ / _oDFoodZoo_ * _wDConsZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	DW_detritus_consumption_by_zooplankton
_wDConsDiatZoo_	_wDConsDiatZoo_ = _cPrefDiat_*_sDDiatW_ / _oDFoodZoo_ * _wDConsZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	DW_diatoms_consumption_by_zooplankton
_wDConsGrenZoo_	_wDConsGrenZoo_ = _cPrefGren_*_sDGrenW_ / _oDFoodZoo_ * _wDConsZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	DW_greens_consumption_by_zooplankton
_wDConsBlueZoo_	_wDConsBlueZoo_ = _cPrefBlue_*_sDBlueW_ / _oDFoodZoo_ * _wDConsZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	DW_blue-greens_consumption_by_zooplankton
_wDConsPhytZoo_	_wDConsPhytZoo_ = _wDConsDiatZoo_ + _wDConsGrenZoo_ + _wDConsBlueZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Phytoplankton_consumption_by_zooplankton
_wDEgesZoo_	_wDEgesZoo_ = _wDConsZoo_ - _wDAssZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Egestion_of_zooplankton
_aCorDRespZoo_	_aCorDRespZoo_ = _MAX_(_cPDZooRef_ / _rPDZoo_,_cNDZooRef_ / _rNDZoo_)	_-_	Corr_factor_of_zoopl_respiration_for_P_and_N_content
_wDRespZoo_	_wDRespZoo_ = _aCorDRespZoo_ * _ukDRespTmZoo_ * _sDZoo_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Zoopl_respiration

_tSiDredDetS_	_tSiDredDetS_ = _akDred_ * _sSiDetS_	_gSi_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_Si_Det_in_lake_sediment

_bRhoSolidSoil_	_bRhoSolidSoil_ = _fDOrgSoil_ * _cRhoOM_ +(1.0 - _fDOrgSoil_) * _cRhoIM_	_g_/_m3_	Average_solid_density_of_soil_material
_tDDredNetSoil_	_tDDredNetSoil_ = -(_tDDredDetS_ / _cRhoOM_) * _bRhoSolidSoil_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_NetSoil_in_lake_sediment
_tDDredNetIMS_	_tDDredNetIMS_ = (1.0 - _fDOrgSoil_) * _tDDredNetSoil_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_NetIMS_in_lake_sediment
_tDDredNetHumS_	_tDDredNetHumS_ = _fDOrgSoil_ * _tDDredNetSoil_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_NetHum_in_lake_sediment
_tPDredNetHumS_	_tPDredNetHumS_ = _cPDSoilOM_ * _tDDredNetHumS_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_P_NetHum_in_lake_sediment
_tNDredNetHumS_	_tNDredNetHumS_ = _cNDSoilOM_ * _tDDredNetHumS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_N_NetHum_in_lake_sediment
_tDDredDiatS_	_tDDredDiatS_ = _akDred_ * _sDDiatS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_Diat_on_lake_sediment
_tPDredDiatS_	_tPDredDiatS_ = _akDred_ * _sPDiatS_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_P_Diat_on_lake_sediment
_tNDredDiatS_	_tNDredDiatS_ = _akDred_ * _sNDiatS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_N_Diat_on_lake_sediment
_tDDredGrenS_	_tDDredGrenS_ = _akDred_ * _sDGrenS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_Gren_on_lake_sediment
_tPDredGrenS_	_tPDredGrenS_ = _akDred_ * _sPGrenS_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_P_Gren_on_lake_sediment
_tNDredGrenS_	_tNDredGrenS_ = _akDred_ * _sNGrenS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_N_Gren_on_lake_sediment
_tDDredBlueS_	_tDDredBlueS_ = _akDred_ * _sDBlueS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_Blue_on_lake_sediment
_tPDredBlueS_	_tPDredBlueS_ = _akDred_ * _sPBlueS_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_P_Blue_on_lake_sediment
_tNDredBlueS_	_tNDredBlueS_ = _akDred_ * _sNBlueS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_N_Blue_on_lake_sediment
_tDDredPhytS_	_tDDredPhytS_ = _tDDredDiatS_+_tDDredGrenS_+_tDDredBlueS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_Phyt_on_lake_sediment
_tPDredPhytS_	_tPDredPhytS_ = _tPDredDiatS_+_tPDredGrenS_+_tPDredBlueS_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_P_Phyt_on_lake_sediment
_tNDredPhytS_	_tNDredPhytS_ = _tNDredDiatS_+_tNDredGrenS_+_tNDredBlueS_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_N_Phyt_on_lake_sediment
_tDDredBent_	_tDDredBent_ = _IF_ (_InclWeb_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _akDredBent_ * _sDBent_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_Bent_on_lake_sediment
_tPDredBent_	_tPDredBent_ = _IF_ (_InclWeb_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _akDredBent_ * _sPBent_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_P_Bent_on_lake_sediment
_tNDredBent_	_tNDredBent_ = _IF_ (_InclWeb_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ _akDredBent_ * _sNBent_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_N_Bent_on_lake_sediment
_tDDredVeg_	_tDDredVeg_ = _akDred_ * _sDVeg_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_DW_Veg_on_lake_sediment
_tPDredVeg_	_tPDredVeg_ = _akDred_ * _sPVeg_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_P_Veg_on_lake_sediment
_tNDredVeg_	_tNDredVeg_ = _akDred_ * _sNVeg_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Dredging_flux_of_N_Veg_on_lake_sediment
_tDDredNetTot_	_tDDredNetTot_ = _tDDredDetS_ - _tDDredNetSoil_ + _tDDredPhytS_ + _tDDredBent_ + _tDDredVeg_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Total_DW_dredging_flux
_tPDredNetTot_	_tPDredNetTot_ = _tPDredDetS_ - _tPDredNetHumS_ + _tPDredAIMS_ + _tPDredPhytS_ + _tPDredBent_ + _tPDredVeg_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Total_P_dredging_flux
_tNDredNetTot_	_tNDredNetTot_ = _tNDredDetS_ - _tNDredNetHumS_ + _tNDredPhytS_ + _tNDredBent_ + _tNDredVeg_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Total_N_dredging_flux
_tSiDredTot_	_tSiDredTot_ = _tSiDredDetS_ + _cSiDDiat_ * _tDDredDiatS_	_gSi_/_m2_/_day_	Total_Si_dredging_flux
_tDIMS_	_tDIMS_ = _tDAbioIMS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Increase_in_inorganic_matter_in_sediment
_tDHumS_	_tDHumS_ = _tDAbioHumS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Increase_in_sediment_humus_in_lake
_tDDetS_	_tDDetS_ = _tDAbioDetS_ + _tDPrimDetS_ + _tDWebDetS_ + _tDBedDetS_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Increase_in_sediment_detritus_in_lake
_vDeltaS_	_vDeltaS_ = (_tDIMS_ / _cRhoIM_ +(_tDHumS_ + _tDDetS_) / _cRhoOM_)/(1.0 - _bPorS_)	_m_/_day_	Turnover_depth_in_lake
_tDBurIM_	_tDBurIM_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ ((_tDHumS_ + _tDDetS_) +(_cRhoOM_ / _cRhoIM_) * _tDIMS_) / ((_sDHumS_ + _sDDetS_) / _sDIMS_ + _cRhoOM_ / _cRhoIM_) _ELSE_ ((_tDHumS_ + _tDDetS_) +(_cRhoOM_ / _cRhoIM_) * _tDIMS_) / (_fDOrgSoil_ /(1.0 - _fDOrgSoil_) + _cRhoOM_ / _cRhoIM_) _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_DW_in_inorganic_matter_in_lake
_tDBurOM_	_tDBurOM_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ (_sDHumS_ + _sDDetS_) / _sDIMS_ * _tDBurIM_ _ELSE_ _fDOrgSoil_ /(1.0 - _fDOrgSoil_) * _tDBurIM_ _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_DW_in_organic_matter_in_lake
_tDBurDet_	_tDBurDet_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _sDDetS_ /(_sDHumS_ + _sDDetS_) * _tDBurOM_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_DW_in_detritus_in_lake
_tDBurHum_	_tDBurHum_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _tDBurOM_ - _tDBurDet_ _ELSE_ _tDBurOM_ _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_DW_in_humus_in_lake
_tDBurTot_	_tDBurTot_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _tDBurIM_ + _tDBurOM_ _ELSE_ _tDBurIM_ + _tDBurOM_ _ENDIF_	_gDW_/_m2_/_day_	Total_DW_burial_flux_in_lake
_tPBurHum_	_tPBurHum_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _rPDHumS_ * _tDBurHum_ _ELSE_ _cPDSoilOM_ * _tDBurHum_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_P_in_humus_in_lake
_tPBurDet_	_tPBurDet_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _rPDDetS_ * _tDBurDet_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_P_in_detritus_in_lake
_tPBurAIM_	_tPBurAIM_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _sPAIMS_ / _sDIMS_ * _tDBurIM_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_P_absorbed_onto_inorganic_matter_in_lake
_tPBurPO4_	_tPBurPO4_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _sPO4S_ *(_vDeltaS_ / _cDepthS_) _ELSE_ _cPO4Ground_ *(_bPorS_ * _vDeltaS_) _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_dissolved_P_in_lake
_tPBurTot_	_tPBurTot_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _tPBurDet_ + _tPBurHum_ + _tPBurAIM_ + _tPBurPO4_ _ELSE_ _tPBurHum_ + _tPBurAIM_ + _tPBurPO4_ _ENDIF_	_gP_/_m2_/_day_	Total_P_burial_flux_in_lake
_tNBurHum_	_tNBurHum_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _rNDHumS_ * _tDBurHum_ _ELSE_ _cNDSoilOM_ * _tDBurHum_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_N_in_humus_in_lake
_tNBurDet_	_tNBurDet_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _rNDDetS_ * _tDBurDet_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_N_in_detritus_in_lake
_tNBurNH4_	_tNBurNH4_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _sNH4S_ *(_vDeltaS_ / _cDepthS_) _ELSE_ _cNH4Ground_ *(_bPorS_ * _vDeltaS_) _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_dissolved_NH4_in_lake
_tNBurNO3_	_tNBurNO3_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _sNO3S_ *(_vDeltaS_ / _cDepthS_) _ELSE_ _cNO3Ground_ *(_bPorS_ * _vDeltaS_) _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_dissolved_NO3_in_lake
_tNBurTot_	_tNBurTot_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _tNBurDet_ + _tNBurHum_ + _tNBurNH4_ + _tNBurNO3_ _ELSE_ _tNBurHum_ + _tNBurNH4_ + _tNBurNO3_ _ENDIF_	_gN_/_m2_/_day_	Total_N_burial_flux_in_lake
_tSiBurDet_	_tSiBurDet_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _rSiDDetS_ * _tDBurDet_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gSi_/_m2_/_day_	Burial_flux_of_Si_in_detritus_in_lake
_tSiBurTot_	_tSiBurTot_ = _IF_ (_vDeltaS_ _GE_ 0.0) _THEN_ _tSiBurDet_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_gSi_/_m2_/_day_	Total_Si_burial_flux_in_lake
_vDeltaW_	_vDeltaW_ = _IF_ (_ConstDepth_ _EQ_ _TRUE_) _THEN_ 0.0 _ELSE_ - _vDeltaS_ _ENDIF_	_m_/_day_	Lake_water_depth_change
_aRelDeltaW_	_aRelDeltaW_ = (_vDeltaW_ + _vDredDepthW_) / _sDepthW_	1/_day_	Relative_water_depth_change_due_to_sediment_turnover_AND_dredging
_tDMarsTotT_	_tDMarsTotT_ = _IF_ (_InclMarsh_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _fMarsh_ _GT_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ (- _tDBurTotM_ - _wDMinDetWM_ * _sDepthWM_ -(1.0 - _fRefrDetS_) * _tDMinDetSM_ - _tDMinHumSM_ + _tDProdPhra_ - _tDRespShootPhra_ - _tDRespRootPhra_ - _tDManShootPhra_) * _fMarsh_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_g_/_m2lake_/_day_	Mass_balance_totals_of_DW_marsh_water_and_vegetation_module
_tPMarsTotT_	_tPMarsTotT_ = _IF_ (_InclMarsh_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _fMarsh_ _GT_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ (- _tPInfPO4SM_ - _tPDifGroundPO4M_ - _tPBurTotM_ - _tPChemPO4M_ - _tPManShootPhra_) * _fMarsh_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_g_/_m2lake_/_day_	Mass_balance_totals_of_P_marsh_water_and_vegetation_module
_tNMarsTotT_	_tNMarsTotT_ = _IF_ (_InclMarsh_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _fMarsh_ _GT_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ (- _tNInfNH4SM_ - _tNInfNO3SM_ - _tNDifGroundNO3M_ - _tNDifGroundNH4M_ - _tNBurTotM_ - _wNDenitWM_ * _sDepthWM_ - _tNDenitSM_ - _tNManShootPhra_) * _fMarsh_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_g_/_m2lake_/_day_	Mass_balance_totals_of_N_marsh_water_and_vegetation_module
_tSiMarsTotT_	_tSiMarsTotT_ = _IF_ (_InclMarsh_ _EQ_ _TRUE_ _AND_ _fMarsh_ _GT_ _NearZero_) _THEN_ - _tSiBurDetM_ * _fMarsh_ _ELSE_ 0.0 _ENDIF_	_g_/_m2lake_/_day_	Mass_balance_totals_of_SI_marsh_water_and_vegetation_module
_aDTotT_	_aDTotT_ = (_sDIMW_+_sDDetW_+_sDDiatW_+_sDGrenW_+_sDBlueW_+_sDZoo_) * _sDepthW_ +_aDFish_+_sDPisc_+_aDVeg_ +_sDIMS_+_sDHumS_+_sDDetS_+_sDDiatS_+_sDGrenS_+_sDBlueS_+_sDBent_ + _aDTotM_	_gDW_/_m2_	Total_DW_in_system
_aNTotT_	_aNTotT_ = (_sNH4W_+_sNO3W_+_sNDetW_+_sNDiatW_+_sNGrenW_+_sNBlueW_ +_sNZoo_)*_sDepthW_ +_aNFish_+_aNPisc_+_aNVeg_ +_sNH4S_+_sNO3S_+_sNDetS_+_sNHumS_+_sNDiatS_+_sNGrenS_+_sNBlueS_ +_sNBent_ + _aNTotM_	_gN_/_m2_	Total_N_in_system
_aPTotT_	_aPTotT_ = (_sPO4W_+_sPDetW_+_sPDiatW_+_sPGrenW_+_sPBlueW_ +_sPZoo_+_sPAIMW_) * _sDepthW_ +_aPFish_+_aPPisc_+_aPVeg_ +_sPO4S_+_sPDetS_+_sPHumS_+_sPDiatS_+_sPGrenS_+_sPBlueS_ +_sPAIMS_+_sPBent_ + _aPTotM_	_gP_/_m2_	Total_P_in_system
_aSiTotT_	_aSiTotT_ = (_sSiO2W_ + _sSiDetW_ + _cSiDDiat_*_sDDiatW_) *_sDepthW_ + _sSiDetS_ + _cSiDDiat_*_sDDiatS_ + _aSiTotM_	_gSi_/_m2_	Total_Si_in_system
_aDError_	_aDError_ = _aDTotT_ - _sDExtTotT_	_gDW_/_m2_	DW_mass_balance_error
_aNError_	_aNError_ = _aNTotT_ - _sNExtTotT_	_gN_/_m2_	N_mass_balance_error
_aPError_	_aPError_ = _aPTotT_ - _sPExtTotT_	_gP_/_m2_	P_mass_balance_error
_aSiError_	_aSiError_ = _aSiTotT_ - _sSiExtTotT_	_gSi_/_m2_	Si_mass_balance_error
_dDepthW_	_dDepthW_ = _vTranDepthW_ + _vDeltaW_ + _vDredDepthW_	_m_/_day_	Derivative_for_water_depth_change_in_lake_water
_dNH4W_	_dNH4W_ = _wNTranNH4W_ + _wNAbioNH4W_ + _wNPrimNH4W_ + _wNBedNH4W_ + _wNWebNH4W_ + _cNBackLoad_ / _sDepthW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sNH4W_ - _wNExchNH4_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_N_ammonium_in_water_in_lake_water
_dNO3W_	_dNO3W_ = _wNTranNO3W_ + _wNAbioNO3W_ + _wNPrimNO3W_ + _wNBedNO3W_ + _wNWebNO3W_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sNO3W_ - _wNExchNO3_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_N_nitrate_in_water_in_lake_water
_dPO4W_	_dPO4W_ = _wPTranPO4W_ + _wPAbioPO4W_ + _wPPrimPO4W_ + _wPBedPO4W_ + _wPWebPO4W_ + _cPBackLoad_ / _sDepthW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sPO4W_ - _wPExchPO4_	_mgP_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_P_SRP_in_water_in_lake_water
_dPAIMW_	_dPAIMW_ = _wPTranAIMW_ + _wPAbioAIMW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sPAIMW_ - _wPExchAIM_	_mgP_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_P_P-adsorbed_onto_IM_in_water_in_lake_water
_dSiO2W_	_dSiO2W_ = _wSiTranSiO2_ + _wSiAbioSiO2W_ + _wSiPrimSiO2W_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sSiO2W_ - _wSiExchSiO2_	_mgSi_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_Si_dissolved_silica_in_water_in_lake_water
_dO2W_	_dO2W_ = _wO2TranW_ + _wO2AbioW_ + _wO2PrimW_ + _tO2BedW_ / _sDepthW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sO2W_ - _wO2Exch_	_gO2_/_m3_/_day_	Derivative_for_O2_oxygen_in_water_in_lake_water
_dDDetW_	_dDDetW_ = _wDTranDetW_ + _wDAbioDetW_ + _wDPrimDetW_ + _wDBedDetW_ + _wDWebDetW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sDDetW_ - _wDExchDet_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_DW_Detritus_in_lake_water
_dNDetW_	_dNDetW_ = _wNTranDetW_ + _wNAbioDetW_ + _wNPrimDetW_ + _wNBedDetW_ + _wNWebDetW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sNDetW_ - _wNExchDet_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_N_Detritus_in_lake_water
_dPDetW_	_dPDetW_ = _wPTranDetW_ + _wPAbioDetW_ + _wPPrimDetW_ + _wPBedDetW_ + _wPWebDetW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sPDetW_ - _wPExchDet_	_mgP_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_P_Detritus_in_lake_water
_dSiDetW_	_dSiDetW_ = _wSiTranDetW_ + _wSiAbioDetW_ + _wSiPrimDetW_ + _wSiWebDetW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sSiDetW_ - _wSiExchDet_	_mgSi_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_Si_Detritus_in_lake_water
_dDIMW_	_dDIMW_ = _wDTranIMW_ + _wDAbioIMW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sDIMW_ - _wDExchIM_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_DW_inorg_matter_in_water_in_lake_water
_dDDiatW_	_dDDiatW_ = _wDTranDiat_ + _wDPrimDiatW_ + _wDWebDiatW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sDDiatW_ - _wDExchDiat_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_DW_Diatoms_in_lake_water
_dNDiatW_	_dNDiatW_ = _wNTranDiat_ + _wNPrimDiatW_ + _wNWebDiatW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sNDiatW_ - _wNExchDiat_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_N_Diatoms_in_lake_water

_dDGrenW_	_dDGrenW_ = _wDTranGren_ + _wDPrimGrenW_ + _wDWebGrenW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sDGrenW_ - _wDExchGren_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_DW_Greens_in_lake_water
_dNGrenW_	_dNGrenW_ = _wNTranGren_ + _wNPrimGrenW_ + _wNWebGrenW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sNGrenW_ - _wNExchGren_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_N_Greens_in_lake_water
_dPGrenW_	_dPGrenW_ = _wPTranGren_ + _wPPrimGrenW_ + _wPWebGrenW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sPGrenW_ - _wPExchGren_	_mgP_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_P_Greens_in_lake_water
_dDBlueW_	_dDBlueW_ = _wDTranBlue_ + _wDPrimBlueW_ + _wDWebBlueW_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sDBlueW_ - _wDExchBlue_	_mg_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_DW_Bluegreens_in_lake_water

_dNZoo_	_dNZoo_ = _wNTranZoo_ + _wNWebZoo_ - _aRelDeltaW_ * _sNZoo_ - _wNExchZoo_	_mgN_/_l_/_day_	Derivative_for_N_Zooplankton_in_lake_water
